0000000                00000 02080  2168      81.     VCLP     CSECT ,
 USING  SCP,R11                     2170      82.              USING SCP,SCPR                ##
 USING  CLW,R10                     2179      83.              USING CLW,CLWR
                                    2188      84.     *  ENTRY POINT
                                    2189      85.     *
                                    2190      86.     * CLP HAS TWO DISTINCT PARTS:
                                    2191      87.     *        1) THE SESSION BREAK ROUTINES WHICH ARE ENTERED FOR
                                    2192      88.     *            A) LOGON/LOGOFF PROCESSING
                                    2193      89.     *            B) ATTENTION, CLP TIMER AND PROGRAM INTERRUPTS
                                    2194      90.     *            C) PANIC,PAUSE,EXIT,AND COMMAND SVCS FROM THE USER PROGRAM
                                    2195      91.     *
                                    2196      92.     *        2) THE BASIC COMMAND LOOP WHICH ISSUES A READ MODE=EDIT, SCANS
                                    2197      93.     *           THE COMMAND AND RETURNS TO READ THE NEXT COMMAND.
                                    2198      94.     *
                                    2199      95.     *        NOTES ON ADDRESSABILITY: THE SESSION BREAK ROUTINES EITHER
                                    2200      96.     *              RETURN TO THE USER PROGRAM OR BRANCH TO THE COMMAND
                                    2201      97.     *              LOOP. WHEN THE COMMAND LOOP IS ENTERED IT SETS UP ITS
                                    2202      98.     *              OWN BASE REGISTER AND NEVER BRANCHES INTO THE
                                    2203      99.     *              SESSION BREAK ROUTINES.
                                    2204     100.     *
                                    2205     101.              ENTRY STARTUP
 000000 0D70                        2206     102.     STARTUP  BASE  BR
 USING  *,R7
